      • getAmFlowImpact

        public TField getAmFlowImpact()
        Returns the AmFlowImpact

        Field description: Defines the flow generated by this event . The various types of flows are : 1. WCF - This stands for weighted Cash flow . This Cash flow is defined in the transaction as Z type flow. Thisflow is used for adjusting the average invested capital. 2. NCF - This stands for Net Cash flow. This Cash flow is defined in the transaction as an 'S' type flow . Thisrepresents a Silent flow. 3. NONE - This is a NON CASH flow . The cash flow field is not updated for this type of an event. 4. BOTH - This type of event is a normal cashflow , that is it is defined as 'Y' type flow in the TRANSACTION. Validation Rules: Standard Alphanumeric Field Valid Values are NCF, WCF, NONE and BOTH

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AmFlowImpact

      • getCashRemain

        public TField getCashRemain()
        Returns the CashRemain

        Field description: YES/NO field controlling whether the system will automatically assign any unused entitlement to the cash optionof this type of Corporate Action. For some types of multiple option corporate actions (such as a SCRIP Dividend) there will be one - or more -options where the portfolio receives securities and an equivalent cash option. If this flag is set to YES then theuser can select the option they require and any unused holdings (due to the terms of the offer, rounding etc.) willautomatically be used for the cash equivalent. If this field is NO then selecting a particular option will causethe system to use all the holdings on that option, even if there may some part of the holding unused. Validation Rules: Only YES or NO allowed. Mandatory field.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The CashRemain

        Field description: For some Demergers or Spin Offs the original holding is retained but the cost of the original position isapportioned across the resulting securities (including the original holding which will have its cost of positionreduced) according to the market value of each resultant holding at the time of the authorisation of theENTITLEMENT record. If this type of book cost apportionment is required the this field should be set to 'YES'. Note : If this field is set to 'YES' then the original holding will be removed at its original cost andre-applied at the new calculated cost. Validation Rules: Only input of 'YES' or 'NO' allowed. Will default to 'NO'.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The DemergeBookCost

      • getDenomLevel

        public TField getDenomLevel()
        Returns the DenomLevel

        Field description: This field will control the way in which the conversion is done. If this field has been set to 'UNIT' then thesystem will convert the minimum trading unit first and the round the resulting figure. The resulting rounded figurewill be used in calculating the new nominal figure. If the field has been set to nulls or 'HOLDING' the conversion will be done on the nominal figure and theresulting nominal figure will be rounded. Validation Rules: Valid values are 'UNIT' or 'HOLDING' Optional input. If no input then the 'HOLDING' method is chosen.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The DenomLevel

      • getEqualisation

        public TField getEqualisation()
        Returns the Equalisation

        Field description: This field will control whether or not this corporate action requires Equalisation processing. Equalisation is the accrued income included in the price of units purchased during the distribution period whichis refunded as part of a unitholder's first distribution on those units. The accrued income is averaged over thedistribution period, resulting in the same rate of distribution (including equalisation) on all units. Equalisationis, therefore, a capital repayment and is not liable to Income Tax and must be deducted from the cost of the unitsfor Capital Gains Tax purposes. Validation Rules: Optional Only input of YES or No are allowed Default to NO Can be YES only when the following fields are set as follows :- RIGHTS is not Y OPTIONS is not Y REINVEST is not Y SECURITY.UPDATE is not Y CASH is Y

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The Equalisation

      • getInstalDistr

        public TField getInstalDistr()
        Returns the InstalDistr

        Field description: This field allows processing either the Capital Instalment or the Capital distribution event type. This functionality is allowed if the CASH and RETAIN.NOMINAL options are set to YES and the other ones are setto NO. The TAXABLE field should be also set to NO. This functionality is not available in case of accumulation income. If this field is set to DISTRIBUTION then the cash to be distributed will be credited to the customer account atthe authorization of ENTITLEMENT. The cost of positions in SECURITY.POSITION and SC.POS.ASSET will be reduced. If this field is set to INSTALMENT then the cash to be paid will be debited from the customer account at theauthorization of ENTITLEMENT. The cost of position in SECURITY.POSITION and SC.POS.ASSET will be increased. Validation Rules: 2 options are allowed: DISTRIBUTION or INSTALMENT Null is the default value.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The InstalDistr

      • getPreAdviceReq

        public TField getPreAdviceReq()
        Returns the PreAdviceReq

        Field description: Determines whether pre confirmation advices are required by default for this diary type. The default value will be used to update DIARY and ENTITLEMENT records created for this diary type. The default values can be modified at the DIARY and ENTILEMENT level. A value of YES will result in a pre confirmation advice being sent for each entitlement record as it is createdeither on hold or as an unauthorised record. The activity code for a pre confirmation advice as defined on EB.ACTIVITY is SC-0100. If the unauthorised record is subsequently amended or deleted then a pre confirmation amendment advice will begenerated, with activity code SC-0101. The data handed of to the delivery module, which can be used to produce customised advices, is as follows Record1 - Corresponds to the DE.MESSAGE record 1500 Record2 - the ENTITLEMENT record Record3 - the DIARY record Record4 - the SEC.ACC.MASTER record Record5 - the SECURITY.MASTER Master record Record6 to Record9 blank. Record9 can be updated via a user-developed routine as defined in USER.ROUTINE on the relevant EB.ADVICESrecord. N.B. field 3 of record 8 will contain the PRINT.FORMAT value of the relevant EB.ADVICES record. Validation Rules: Must be set to YES or NO

      • getRights

        public TField getRights()
        Returns the Rights

        Field description: Flag to indicate whether any securities will be issued by the diary event which it is being defined. If this field is set to 'Y' then the Corporate Actions being defined in the DIARY.TYPE record is a Rights typeCorporate Action. That is holding a particular security on the Ex Div Date will result in the portfolio beingcredited with a number of tradable items which can then be bought or sold up to the Pay Date of the Event. On thePay Date of the Event the Rights will be converted to another security - usually at a fixed cost per right. If this field is set to 'Y' then for the duration of the event (between ex-div date and pay date) any SEC.TRADEor SECURITY.TRANFER done by a portfolio in the Rights stock will be recorded on the ENTITLEMENT record in theSEC.TRADE.ID, BUY.NUMBER and SELL.NUMBER fields and the amount of stock movement will be taken into account whenthe final Rights holding is converted on pay date. Validation Rules: Allowed values are 'Y'ES/'N'O only. Mandatory input.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The Rights

      • getToleranceNom

        public TField getToleranceNom()
        Returns the ToleranceNom

        Field description: Whole number to define the tolerance while performing reconciliation for Stock Movements can be specifiedhere.This field is applicable for ID as ENTITLEMENT Precedence : DIARY.TYPE > SC.CA.PARAMETER Authorization of Entitlement and Error log updation is based on difference between the recorded value andquantity from 566 as below -

        • No difference - Entitlements will be authorized
        • Within tolerance range - a warning will be recorded in SC.CA.ERROR.LOG , Entitlements will be authorized
        • Exceeds tolerance range - an error will be recorded in SC.CA.ERROR.LOG , Entitlements will not be authorized

      • getUpfrontPayment

        public TField getUpfrontPayment()
        Returns the UpfrontPayment

        Field description: Field to identify if payment is required prior to security movement. If the flag is set to YES , First Authorisation of ENTITLEMENT will debit customer account and second/Consequentauthorisation of ENTITLEMENT will perform security movement.Otherwise , Authorisation of ENTITLEMENT will perform security movement. UPFRONT.PAYMENT criteria follows below logic: If UPFRONT.PAYMENT field in DIARY.TYPE is not YES or DIARY is NO then event is not eligible for upfront payment If UPFRONT.PAYMENT field in DIARY.TYPE is YES and SC.PARAMETER is NO and DIARY is blank then event is noteligible for upfront payment All other cases apart from above are eligible for upfront payment. Validation Rules Input Allowed- YES,NO Allowed input only if UPDATE.NOSTRO is not set to YES

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The UpfrontPayment

        public TField getVerifyRequired()

        Field description: YES/NO field used to control whether this type of Corporate Action needs to be verified. Only input of YES or No is allowed with the field defaulting to NO. If this field is set to YES then any ENTITLEMENT record created for this type of Corporate Action will need tobe accessed with the 'V' (Verify) function before input is allowed. If it is NO then the Entitlement records can be Input or Authorised directly depending on whether theEntitlement record concerned has enough information to have an INAU or IHLD status. All the Entitlement records created by a single Diary record can verified together using the applicationSC.ENT.VERIFY. Validation Rules: Only input of YES or NO allowed. Will default to NO. Mandatory input.

        public void setAmFlowImpact(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for AmFlowImpact
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the flow generated by this event . The various types of flows are : 1. WCF - This stands for weighted Cash flow . This Cash flow is defined in the transaction as Z type flow. Thisflow is used for adjusting the average invested capital. 2. NCF - This stands for Net Cash flow. This Cash flow is defined in the transaction as an 'S' type flow . Thisrepresents a Silent flow. 3. NONE - This is a NON CASH flow . The cash flow field is not updated for this type of an event. 4. BOTH - This type of event is a normal cashflow , that is it is defined as 'Y' type flow in the TRANSACTION. Validation Rules: Standard Alphanumeric Field Valid Values are NCF, WCF, NONE and BOTH

      • setCashRemain

        public void setCashRemain(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for CashRemain
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: YES/NO field controlling whether the system will automatically assign any unused entitlement to the cash optionof this type of Corporate Action. For some types of multiple option corporate actions (such as a SCRIP Dividend) there will be one - or more -options where the portfolio receives securities and an equivalent cash option. If this flag is set to YES then theuser can select the option they require and any unused holdings (due to the terms of the offer, rounding etc.) willautomatically be used for the cash equivalent. If this field is NO then selecting a particular option will causethe system to use all the holdings on that option, even if there may some part of the holding unused. Validation Rules: Only YES or NO allowed. Mandatory field.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setEqualisation

        public void setEqualisation(TField value)
        Set the specified value for Equalisation
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field will control whether or not this corporate action requires Equalisation processing. Equalisation is the accrued income included in the price of units purchased during the distribution period whichis refunded as part of a unitholder's first distribution on those units. The accrued income is averaged over thedistribution period, resulting in the same rate of distribution (including equalisation) on all units. Equalisationis, therefore, a capital repayment and is not liable to Income Tax and must be deducted from the cost of the unitsfor Capital Gains Tax purposes. Validation Rules: Optional Only input of YES or No are allowed Default to NO Can be YES only when the following fields are set as follows :- RIGHTS is not Y OPTIONS is not Y REINVEST is not Y SECURITY.UPDATE is not Y CASH is Y

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setFactorPayment

        public void setFactorPayment(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for FactorPayment
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field will be used to specify whether or not for bonds with factors an extra payment needs to be made to thecustomer for a factor change. The field can be set to 'Y' in the case of Mortgage Backed Securities where adecreasing factor will be paid out to the customer as an extra payment. If this action coincides with the couponpayment which will be the case in most cases the system will raise two separate accounting entries for the customerand a single entry for the depository. This field has no default setting and if an existing record is amended then the input will be required. In thiscase NO should be used as this is functionally equivalent to the existing setting of blank. Validation Rules: Mandatory Input Valid values in the field are 'Y' or 'NO'.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setInstalDistr

        public void setInstalDistr(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for InstalDistr
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field allows processing either the Capital Instalment or the Capital distribution event type. This functionality is allowed if the CASH and RETAIN.NOMINAL options are set to YES and the other ones are setto NO. The TAXABLE field should be also set to NO. This functionality is not available in case of accumulation income. If this field is set to DISTRIBUTION then the cash to be distributed will be credited to the customer account atthe authorization of ENTITLEMENT. The cost of positions in SECURITY.POSITION and SC.POS.ASSET will be reduced. If this field is set to INSTALMENT then the cash to be paid will be debited from the customer account at theauthorization of ENTITLEMENT. The cost of position in SECURITY.POSITION and SC.POS.ASSET will be increased. Validation Rules: 2 options are allowed: DISTRIBUTION or INSTALMENT Null is the default value.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void setOverdueDays(TField value)
        Set the specified value for OverdueDays
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Number of Days after the date in the OVERDUE.DATE field after which this type of Corporate Action would beoverdue. This field in conjunction with the OVERDUE.DATE field can be used to report ENTITLEMENT records that are stillunauthorised after the 'overdue' date for the event. The enquiry OVERDUE.EVENTS can be used as an example enquiryfor reporting overdue events. If for example this field contained 5 and the OVERDUE.DATE field contained VALUE.DATE then if an ENTITLEMENTrecord value dated 21st March 1996 was still unauthorised after the 26th March then it would be considered overdue. Validation Rules: Numeric and mandatory input.

      • setPreAdviceReq

        public void setPreAdviceReq(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for PreAdviceReq
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Determines whether pre confirmation advices are required by default for this diary type. The default value will be used to update DIARY and ENTITLEMENT records created for this diary type. The default values can be modified at the DIARY and ENTILEMENT level. A value of YES will result in a pre confirmation advice being sent for each entitlement record as it is createdeither on hold or as an unauthorised record. The activity code for a pre confirmation advice as defined on EB.ACTIVITY is SC-0100. If the unauthorised record is subsequently amended or deleted then a pre confirmation amendment advice will begenerated, with activity code SC-0101. The data handed of to the delivery module, which can be used to produce customised advices, is as follows Record1 - Corresponds to the DE.MESSAGE record 1500 Record2 - the ENTITLEMENT record Record3 - the DIARY record Record4 - the SEC.ACC.MASTER record Record5 - the SECURITY.MASTER Master record Record6 to Record9 blank. Record9 can be updated via a user-developed routine as defined in USER.ROUTINE on the relevant EB.ADVICESrecord. N.B. field 3 of record 8 will contain the PRINT.FORMAT value of the relevant EB.ADVICES record. Validation Rules: Must be set to YES or NO

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setReinvest

        public void setReinvest(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for Reinvest
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Flag to indicate whether any cash offered can be reinvested in the original security. This flag should be set to 'Y' if the Corporate Action being defined is a re-investment corporate action. Thatis one where the dividend (or coupon) received from the holding of a particular security is reinvested in thatsecurity. The resultant ENTITLEMENT records will calculate the amount to be received by the portfolio and thenumber of securities that can be purchased with that amount of cash at the current market price of the securityfrom the SECURITY.MASTER record that defines the security. Validation Rules: Allowed values are 'Y'ES/'N'O only. Mandatory input.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setRights

        public void setRights(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for Rights
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Flag to indicate whether any securities will be issued by the diary event which it is being defined. If this field is set to 'Y' then the Corporate Actions being defined in the DIARY.TYPE record is a Rights typeCorporate Action. That is holding a particular security on the Ex Div Date will result in the portfolio beingcredited with a number of tradable items which can then be bought or sold up to the Pay Date of the Event. On thePay Date of the Event the Rights will be converted to another security - usually at a fixed cost per right. If this field is set to 'Y' then for the duration of the event (between ex-div date and pay date) any SEC.TRADEor SECURITY.TRANFER done by a portfolio in the Rights stock will be recorded on the ENTITLEMENT record in theSEC.TRADE.ID, BUY.NUMBER and SELL.NUMBER fields and the amount of stock movement will be taken into account whenthe final Rights holding is converted on pay date. Validation Rules: Allowed values are 'Y'ES/'N'O only. Mandatory input.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setRoundingLevel

        public void setRoundingLevel(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for RoundingLevel
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: New field that will control the level at which the ROUNDING takes place. This will be an optional field. Validinput will be 'CUSTOMER', 'DEPOSITORY'. The default will be 'CUSTOMER'. At the 'DEPOSITORY' level, the rounding can be 'STANDARD' or 'DOWN'. The 'STANDARD' option means a standardadjustment. The 'DOWN' option allows pro-rating the unallocated securities and cash remaining to customers withfractions. When ROUNDING.LEVEL is set to DEPO.RERUN, then excess nominal or cash received from depository will be distributedto entitlements when Diary is rerun with DEPO.ADJUST field enabled Validation Rules: Valid inputs are 'CUSTOMER' or 'DEPOSITORY', 'DEPO.RERUN' Default will be 'CUSTOMER' ROUNDING.LEVEL can be set to DEPO.RERUN only1) when either Cash rounding method or Nom rounding method is set to DN2) when CASH is set to Yes or FREE.SECURITIES is set to Yes in DIARY.TYPE

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setToleranceNom

        public void setToleranceNom(TField value)
        Set the specified value for ToleranceNom
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Whole number to define the tolerance while performing reconciliation for Stock Movements can be specifiedhere.This field is applicable for ID as ENTITLEMENT Precedence : DIARY.TYPE > SC.CA.PARAMETER Authorization of Entitlement and Error log updation is based on difference between the recorded value andquantity from 566 as below -

        • No difference - Entitlements will be authorized
        • Within tolerance range - a warning will be recorded in SC.CA.ERROR.LOG , Entitlements will be authorized
        • Exceeds tolerance range - an error will be recorded in SC.CA.ERROR.LOG , Entitlements will not be authorized

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

Diary will notbe updated automatically and update to DIARY will be manual process

      • setUpdateNostro

        public void setUpdateNostro(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for UpdateNostro
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: YES/NO field controlling whether or not the system will directly update the nostro account for the depositoryside accounting entries or only the suspense account identified in the SUSPENSE.ACCOUNT field. If this field is YES then the Nostro Account will be updated. If this field is NO then the Suspense Account will be updated. Validation Rules: Only input of YES or NO allowed. Will default to YES. Mandatory input. Once the DIARY.TYPE record has been authorised then this field cannot be changed.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setUpfrontPayment

        public void setUpfrontPayment(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for UpfrontPayment
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Field to identify if payment is required prior to security movement. If the flag is set to YES , First Authorisation of ENTITLEMENT will debit customer account and second/Consequentauthorisation of ENTITLEMENT will perform security movement.Otherwise , Authorisation of ENTITLEMENT will perform security movement. UPFRONT.PAYMENT criteria follows below logic: If UPFRONT.PAYMENT field in DIARY.TYPE is not YES or DIARY is NO then event is not eligible for upfront payment If UPFRONT.PAYMENT field in DIARY.TYPE is YES and SC.PARAMETER is NO and DIARY is blank then event is noteligible for upfront payment All other cases apart from above are eligible for upfront payment. Validation Rules Input Allowed- YES,NO Allowed input only if UPDATE.NOSTRO is not set to YES

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setVerifyRequired

        public void setVerifyRequired(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for VerifyRequired
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: YES/NO field used to control whether this type of Corporate Action needs to be verified. Only input of YES or No is allowed with the field defaulting to NO. If this field is set to YES then any ENTITLEMENT record created for this type of Corporate Action will need tobe accessed with the 'V' (Verify) function before input is allowed. If it is NO then the Entitlement records can be Input or Authorised directly depending on whether theEntitlement record concerned has enough information to have an INAU or IHLD status. All the Entitlement records created by a single Diary record can verified together using the applicationSC.ENT.VERIFY. Validation Rules: Only input of YES or NO allowed. Will default to NO. Mandatory input.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing
